[1/35] CQ04: Which of the named and published algorithms does this tool use?
======================================================================
<?xml version="1.0"?>
<rdf:RDF xml:base="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"
         xmlns:owl="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
         xmlns:rdf="http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#"
         xmlns:rdfs="http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#"
         xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#">

  <owl:Ontology rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#"/>

  <!-- owl:Class declarations -->

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A software tool that processes data using algorithms.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Tool</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

<owl:Class rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">A named and published computational procedure.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">Algorithm</rdfs:label>
</owl:Class>

  <!-- owl:ObjectProperty declarations -->

<owl:ObjectProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#usesAlgorithm">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Indicates that a tool uses an algorithm.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">uses algorithm</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Tool"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
</owl:ObjectProperty>

  <!-- owl:DatatypeProperty declarations -->

<owl:DatatypeProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#algorithmName">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">The name of the algorithm.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">algorithm name</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#xsd:string"/>
</owl:DatatypeProperty>

<owl:DatatypeProperty rdf:about="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#algorithmPublished">
  <rdfs:comment xml:lang="en">Whether the algorithm has been published.</rdfs:comment>
  <rdfs:label xml:lang="en">algorithm published</rdfs:label>
  <rdfs:domain rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#Algorithm"/>
  <rdfs:range rdf:resource="http://www.semanticweb.org/myontology#xsd:boolean"/>
</owl:DatatypeProperty>

</rdf:RDF>

</owl:Class>
